spawn(function() repeat wait() until game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild('RobloxPromptGui')
local lp,po,ts = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer,game.CoreGui.RobloxPromptGui.promptOverlay,game:GetService('TeleportService')
po.ChildAdded:connect(function(a)
if a.Name == 'ErrorPrompt' then
repeat task.wait(5) pcall(function()
for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(game:HttpGetAsync("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100")).data) do
if type(v) == "table" and v.maxPlayers > v.playing and v.ping < 150 and v.id ~= game.JobId then
game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, v.id)
end end end)
until cum == true
end
end)
end)

repeat wait() until game:IsLoaded()

function AntiMod() 
game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("UserData"):WaitForChild("User_".._G.Mod.UserId):WaitForChild("FinishedLoading"):GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function() 
local WBH = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/1099436799539019807/t7mSIrJNimbbM2XrxDaFdn0MOWRNLXwP7UWui-BmUj5W6TTuj7ClL_NEpVZ7bdpLA2zS"
local Data ={["content"] = _G.Mod.Name.." Mod/Snitch is playing ||@everyone||"}
local Headers = {["Content-Type"]="application/json"}
local Encoded = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONEncode(Data)
Request = http_request or request or HttpPost or syn.request
local Final = {Url = WBH, Body = Encoded, Method = "POST", Headers = Headers}
Request(Final)
Lp:Kick(_G.Mod.Name.." in Server")
end)
end
